ржкрзНрж░рж╛ржЗржоржнрж╛ржбрж╛ ржмрж┐ржбрж╝рж▓рж╛ ржмрзГрждрзНрждрж┐ рзирзжрзирзж ржПрж░ ржЖржмрзЗржжржиржкрждрзНрж░ ржбрж╛ржЙржирж▓рзЛржб ржХрж░рзБржи┬а–┬аржПржЦрж╛ржирзЗ ржХрзНрж▓рж┐ржХ ржХрж░рзБржи

Step 1: At first download the Priyamvada Birla Scholarship рзирзжрзирзж Application Form. This form available on the official website of South Point School (link is given below).

Step 2:┬аFill the complete Application Form clearly with your Personal Details, Address, Academic Details, Family Income Details & Declaration. Now attach the following self-attested documents with this application form.

  1. Recent Colour Photograph (Paste on the Form)
  2. Madhyamik Marksheet.
  3. Higher Secondary Marksheet.
  4. Rank Card (if any).
  5. Proof of admission in Institute.

Step 3:┬аSubmit this filled Application Form to the Head of your current Institution / College.

Step 4:┬аThe Head of the Institution will forward the application form to this following address,

The Board of Trustees, Madhav Prasad Birla Apex Charitable Trust, c/o South Point High School, 82/7A, Ballygunge Place, Kolkata 700019.
